\\\\: \\\\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\\\\\\n166:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   -\\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\\\\\\n167:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n168:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow            &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                   \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n179:             &\\\\hspace{15mm} g_t  \\\\leftarrow  \\\\textbf{b}_t   \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n183:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n184:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n185: \\n186:     Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\\n187:     `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\\n188:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n189:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n190:     Args:\\n191:         {_params_doc}\\n192:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\\n193:         momentum (float, optional): momentum factor (default: 0)\\n194:         dampening (float, This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. momentum is based on the formula from\\n187:     `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\\n188:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n189:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n190:     Args:\\n191:         {_params_doc}\\n192:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\\n193:         momentum (float, optional): momentum factor (default: 0)\\n194:         dampening (float, This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. \n186:     Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\n187:     `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\n188:     \"\"\"\n189:     + rf\"\"\"\n190:     Args:\n191: optional): dampening for momentum (default: 0)\n195:         weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n196:         nesterov (bool, optional): enables Nesterov momentum. Only applicable\n197:             when momentum is non-zero. (default: False)\n198:         {_maximize_doc}\n199:         {_foreach_doc}\n200:         {_differentiable_doc}\n201:         {_fused_doc}\n202:     \"\"\"\n203:     + r\"\"\"\n204: \n205:     Example:\n206:         >>> # xdoctest: +SKIP\n207:         >>> optimizer = torch.optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.1, momentum=0.9)\n208:         >>> optimizer.zero_grad()\n209:         >>> loss_fn(model(input), target).backward()\n210:         >>> optimizer.step()\n211: \n212:     __ http://www.cs.toronto.edu/%7Ehinton/absps/momentum.pdf\n213: \n214:     .. note::\n215:         The implementation of SGD with Momentum/Nesterov subtly differs from\n216:         Sutskever et al. and implementations in some other frameworks.\n217: \n218:         Considering the specific case of Momentum, the update can be written as\n219: \n220:         .. math::\n221:             \\begin{aligned}\n222:                 v_{t+1} & = \\mu * v_{t} + g_{t+1}, \\\\\n223:                 p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - \\text{lr} * v_{t+1},\n224:             \\end{aligned}\n225: \n226:         where :math:`p`, :math:`g`, :math:`v` and :math:`\\mu` denote the\n227:         parameters, gradient, velocity, and momentum respectively.\n228: \n229:         This is in contrast to Sutskever et al. and\n230:         other frameworks which employ an update of the form\n231: \n232:         .. math::\n233:             \\begin{aligned}\n234:                 v_{t+1} & = \\mu * v_{t} + \\text{lr} * g_{t+1}, \\\\\n235:                 p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - v_{t+1}.\n236:             \\end{aligned}\n237: \n238:         The Nesterov version is analogously modified.\n239: \n240:         Moreover, the initial value of the momentum buffer is set to the\n241:         gradient value at the first step. This is in contrast to some other\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\n245: \n246:     \"\"\"\n247: )\n248: \n249: \n250: def sgd(\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n261:     *,\n262:     weight_decay: float,\n263:     momentum: float,\n264:     lr: float,\n265:     dampening: float,\n266:     nesterov: bool,\n267:     maximize: bool,\n268: ):\n269:     r\"\"\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\n270: \n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\n272:     \"\"\"\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. \\n273: \\n274: Adam.__doc__ = (\\n275:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Implements Adam algorithm.\\n276: \\n277:     .. math::\\n278:        \\\\begin{aligned}\\n279:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n280:             &\\\\textbf{input}      : \\\\gamma \\\\text{ (lr)}, \\\\beta_1, \\\\beta_2\\n281:                 \\\\text{ (betas)},\\\\theta_0 \\\\text{ (params)},f(\\\\theta) \\\\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\\\\\\n282:             &\\\\hspace{13mm}      \\\\lambda \\\\text{ (weight decay)},  \\\\: \\\\textit{amsgrad},\\n283:                 \\\\:\\\\textit{maximize},  \\\\: \\\\epsilon \\\\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\\\\\\n284:             &\\\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\\\leftarrow 0 \\\\text{ ( first moment)},\\n285:                 v_0\\\\leftarrow 0 \\\\text{ (second moment)},\\\\: v_0^{max}\\\\leftarrow 0          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n286:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n287:             &\\\\textbf{for} \\\\: t=1 \\\\: \\\\textbf{to} \\\\: \\\\ldots \\\\: \\\\textbf{do}                         \\\\\\\\\\n288: \\n289:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\\\\\\n290:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   -\\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\\\\\\n291:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n292:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\\\\\\n293:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\lambda \\\\neq 0                                           \\\\\\\\\\n294:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\\\leftarrow g_t + \\\\lambda  \\\\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\\\\\\n295:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\\\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\\\\\\n296:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\\\\\\n297:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\widehat{m_t} \\\\leftarrow   m_t/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_1^t \\\\big)                   \\\\\\\\\\n298:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\\\\\\n299:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\\\leftarrow \\\\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\\\\\\n300:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_2^t \\\\big)              \\\\\\\\\\n301:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n302:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow   v_t/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_2^t \\\\big)                  \\\\\\\\\\n303:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\theta_t \\\\leftarrow \\\\theta_{t-1} - \\\\gamma \\\\widehat{m_t}/\\n304:                 \\\\big(\\\\sqrt{\\\\widehat{v_t}} + \\\\epsilon \\\\big)                                       \\\\\\\\\\n305:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n306:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t                                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n307:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n308:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n309: \\n310:     For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\\n311:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n312:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n313:     Args:\\n314:         {_params_doc}\\n315:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\\n316:             is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\\n317:             LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\\n318:         betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\\n319:             running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\\n320:         eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\\n321:             numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\\n322:         weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\\n323:         decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\\n324:             equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\\n325:             decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\\n326:         amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\\n327:             algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\\n328:             (default: False)\\n329:         {_foreach_doc}\\n330:         {_maximize_doc}\\n331:         {_capturable_doc}\\n332:         {_differentiable_doc}\\n333:         {_fused_doc}\\n334:     .. \\n345: def _single_tensor_adam(\\n346:     params: list[Tensor],\\n347:     grads: list[Tensor],\\n348:     exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\\n349:     exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\\n350:     max_exp_avg_sqs: &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\lambda \\\\neq 0                                           \\\\\\\\\\n294:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\\\leftarrow g_t + \\\\lambda  \\\\theta_{t-1}       \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\\\\\\n297:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\widehat{m_t} \\\\leftarrow   m_t/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_1^t \\\\big)                   \\\\\\\\\\n298:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\\\\\\n299:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\\\leftarrow \\\\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\\\\\\n300:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_2^t \\\\big)              \\\\\\\\\\n301:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n302:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow   v_t/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_2^t \\\\big)                  \\\\\\\\\\n303:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\theta_t \\\\leftarrow \\\\theta_{t-1} - \\\\gamma \\\\widehat{m_t}/\\n304:                 \\\\big(\\\\sqrt{\\\\widehat{v_t}} + \\\\epsilon \\\\big)                                       \\\\\\\\\\n305:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n306:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t                                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n307:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n308:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n309: \\n310:     For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\\n311:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n312:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n313:     Args:\\n314:         {_params_doc}\\n315:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\\n316:             is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\\n317:             LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\\n318:         betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\\n319:             running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\\n320:         eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\\n321:             numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\\n322:         weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\\n323:         decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\\n324:             equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\\n325:             decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\\n326:         amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\\n327:             algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\\n328:             (default: False)\\n329:         {_foreach_doc}\\n330:         {_maximize_doc}\\n331:         {_capturable_doc}\\n332:         {_differentiable_doc}\\n333:         {_fused_doc}\\n334:     .. \\n345: def _single_tensor_adam(\\n346:     params: list[Tensor],\\n347:     grads: list[Tensor],\\n348:     exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\\n349:     exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\\n350:     max_exp_avg_sqs:        beta1_dict = None\\n388: \\n389:     for i, param in enumerate(params):\\n390:         grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\\n391:         exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\\n392: else:\\n466:             exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\\n467: \\n468:         if capturable or differentiable:\\n469:             step =   else:\\n478:                 bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\\n479: \\n480:             # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\\n481:             if differentiable and step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\\n491: \\n492:             bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\\n493: \\n494:             if amsgrad:\\n495:                 # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\\n496:                 if differentiable:\\n497:                     max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\\n498:                 else:\\n499:           ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\\n513: \\n514:             if differentiable:\\n515:                 param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\\n516:             else:\\n517: _multi_tensor_adam(\\n545:     params: list[Tensor],\\n546:     grads: list[Tensor],\\n547:     exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\\n548:     exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\\n549:     max_exp_avg_sqs:         {beta1.device: beta1}\\n621:         if isinstance(beta1, Tensor) and str(beta1.device) != \\\"cpu\\\"\\n622:         else None\\n623:     )\\n624: \\n625:     for (\\n626: cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\\n636:         device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\\n637:         device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\\n638: \\n639:         device = device_params[0].device\\n640:         if beta1_dict is not None and device not in beta1_dict:\\n641:             beta1_dict[device] = beta1.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr, attr-defined]\\n642: \\n643:         device_beta1 = beta1_dict[device] if beta1_dict else beta1\\n644: \\n645:         # Handle complex parameters\\n646: Update steps\\n665:         # If steps are on CPU, foreach will fall back to the slow path, which is a for-loop calling t.add(1) over\\n666:         # and over. 1 will then be wrapped into a Tensor over and over again, which is slower than if we just\\n667:         # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\\n668:         if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and device_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\\n669:             torch._foreach_add_(\\n670:                 device_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\\\"cpu\\\"), alpha=1.0\\n671:             )\\n672:         else:\\n673:             torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\\n674: \\n675:         if weight_decay != 0:\\n676:             if decoupled_weight_decay:\\n677:                 # Perform stepweight decay\\n678:                 torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\\n679:             else:\\n680:                 # Reuse the intermediate memory (device_grads) already allocated for maximize\\n681:                 if maximize:\\n682:                     torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\\n683:                 else:\\n684:                     device_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[assignment]\\n685:                         device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\\n686:                     )\\n687: \\n688:         # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\\n689:         # Due to the strictness of the _foreach_addcmul API, we can't have a single\\n698:         # tensor scalar as the scalar arg (only python number is supported there)\\n699:         # as a result, separate out the value mul\\n700:         # Filed https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/139795\\n701:         if isinstance(beta2, torch.Tensor):\\n702:             scaled_device_grads = torch._foreach_mul(device_grads, 1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[assignment]\\n703:             value = 1.0\\n704:         else:\\n705:             scaled_device_grads = device_grads  # type: ignore[assignment]\\n706:             value = 1 - beta2\\n707: \\n708:         torch._foreach_addcmul_(\\n709:             device_exp_avg_sqs, scaled_device_grads, device_grads, value\\n710:         )\\n711: \\n712:         # Delete the local intermediate(s) since they won't be used anymore to save on peak memory\\n713:         del device_grads\\n714:         del scaled_device_grads\\n715: \\n716:         bias_correction1: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\\n717:         bias_correction2: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\\n718:         bias_correction2_sqrt: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\\n719: \\n720:         if capturable:\\n721:             bias_correction1 = torch._foreach_pow(beta1, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\\n722:             bias_correction2 = torch._foreach_pow(beta2, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\\n723:             # foreach_sub doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\\n724:             torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction1, 1)\\n725:             torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction2, 1)\\n726:             # we do not negate bias_correction1 as it'll need to be negated later anyway\\n727:             torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\\n728: \\n729:             # foreach_div doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\\n730:             torch._foreach_div_(bias_correction1, lr)\\n731:             torch._foreach_reciprocal_(bias_correction1)\\n732: \\n733:             torch._foreach_sqrt_(bias_correction2)\\n734: \\n735:             # Re-assign for clarity as we maintain minimal intermediates: we'll have\\n736:             # step_size = - lr / (1 - beta1 ^ t) where t = num_steps\\n737:             # bias_correction2_sqrt = sqrt(1 - beta2 ^ t)\\n738:             step_size = bias_correction1\\n739:             bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2\\n740: \\n741:             if amsgrad:\\n742:                 device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\\n743:                 # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\\n744:                 torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)  # type: ignore[assignment]\\n745: \\n746:                 # Set intermediate to the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient when amsgrad\\n747:                 exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\\n748:             else:\\n749:                 exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\\n750: \\n751:             torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\\n752:             torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\\n753:             torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, step_size)\\n754: \\n755:             # at this point, exp_avg_sq_sqrt = - (1 - beta^t) * [sqrt(exp_avg_sq / (1 - beta2^t)) + eps] / lr\\n756:             torch._foreach_addcdiv_(device_params, device_exp_avgs, exp_avg_sq_sqrt)\\n757:         else:\\n758:             bias_correction1 = [\\n759:                 1 - beta1 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\\n760:             ]\\n761:             bias_correction2 = [\\n762:                 1 - beta2 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\\n763:             ]\\n764: \\n765:             step_size = _stack_if_compiling([(lr / bc) * -1 for bc in bias_correction1])\\n766: \\n767:             bias_correction2_sqrt = [bc**0.5 for bc in bias_correction2]  # type: ignore[arg-type]\\n768: \\n769:             if amsgrad:\\n770:                 device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\\n771:                 # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\\n772:                 torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)\\n773: \\n774:                 # \n277:     .. math::\n278:        \\begin{aligned}\n279:             &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n280:             &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n281:                 \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n282:             &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n283:                 \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n284:             &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n285:                 v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n286:             &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n287:             &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n288: \n289:             &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n290:             &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n291:             &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n292:             &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n293:             &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n294:             &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n295:             &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n296:             &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n297:             &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n298:             &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n299:             &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n300:             &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n301:             &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n302:             &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n303:             &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n304:                 \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n305:             &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n306:             &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n307:             &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n308:        \\end{aligned}\n309: \n310:     For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n311:     \"\"\"\n312:     + rf\"\"\"\n313:     Args:\n314:         {_params_doc}\n315:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n316:             is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n317:             LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n318:         betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n319:             running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n320:         eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n321:             numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n322:         weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n323:         decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n324:             equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n325:             decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n326:         amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n327:             algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n328:             (default: False)\n329:         {_foreach_doc}\n330:         {_maximize_doc}\n331:         {_capturable_doc}\n332:         {_differentiable_doc}\n333:         {_fused_doc}\n334:     .. This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused.             &\\\\textbf{input}      : \\\\gamma \\\\text{ (lr)}, \\\\: \\\\theta_0 \\\\text{ (params)}, \\\\: f(\\\\theta)\\n160:                 \\\\text{ (objective)}, \\\\: \\\\lambda \\\\text{ \\\\\\\\\\n167:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n168:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow            &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                   \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n179:             &\\\\hspace{15mm} g_t  \\\\leftarrow  \\\\textbf{b}_t                                         \\\\\\\\\\n180:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\theta_t \\\\leftarrow \\\\theta_{t-1} - \\\\gamma g_t                    \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n181:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n182:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t                                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n183:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n184:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n185: \\n186:     Nesterov    {_params_doc}\\n192:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\\n193:         momentum (float, optional): momentum factor (default: 0)\\n194:         dampening (float, This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. One notable side effect\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef sgd(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    d_p_list: list[Tensor],\n    momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n    # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n    # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n    has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n    foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n    fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    *,\n    weight_decay: float,\n    momentum: float,\n    lr: float,\n    dampening: float,\n    nesterov: bool,\n    maximize: bool,\n):\n    r\"\"\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\n\n    See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. loss = None\n        if closure is not None:\n            with torch.enable_grad():\n                loss = closure()\n\n        for group in self.param_groups:\n            params_with_grad: list[Tensor] = []\n            grads: list[Tensor] = []\n            exp_avgs: list[Tensor] = []\n            exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor] = []\n            max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor] = []\n            state_steps: list[Tensor] = []\n            beta1, beta2 = group[\"betas\"]\n\n            has_complex = self._init_group(\n                group,\n                params_with_grad,\n                grads,\n                exp_avgs,\n                exp_avg_sqs,\n                max_exp_avg_sqs,\n                state_steps,\n            )\n\n            adam(\n                params_with_grad,\n                grads,\n                exp_avgs,\n                exp_avg_sqs,\n                max_exp_avg_sqs,\n                state_steps,\n                amsgrad=group[\"amsgrad\"],\n                has_complex=has_complex,\n                beta1=beta1,\n                beta2=beta2,\n                lr=group[\"lr\"],\n                weight_decay=group[\"weight_decay\"],\n                eps=group[\"eps\"],\n                maximize=group[\"maximize\"],\n                foreach=group[\"foreach\"],\n                capturable=group[\"capturable\"],\n                differentiable=group[\"differentiable\"],\n                fused=group[\"fused\"],\n                grad_scale=getattr(self, \"grad_scale\", None),\n                found_inf=getattr(self, \"found_inf\", None),\n                decoupled_weight_decay=group[\"decoupled_weight_decay\"],\n            )\n\n        return loss\n\n\nAdam.__doc__ = (\n    r\"\"\"Implements Adam algorithm.\n\n    .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n    else:\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n    else:\n        beta1_dict = None\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n\n            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n            key = (device, dtype)\n            if key not in beta1_dict:\n                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise RuntimeError(\n                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if lr.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n\n    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n            supports_xla=False\n        )\n        assert all(\n            p.device.type == step.device.type\n            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n        ), (\n            f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n        )\n\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n    # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        {beta1.device: beta1}\n        if isinstance(beta1, Tensor) and str(beta1.device) != \"cpu\"\n        else None\n    )\n\n    for (\n        device_params_,\n        device_grads_,\n        device_exp_avgs_,\n        device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_max_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_state_steps_,\n    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n\n        device = device_params[0].device\n        if beta1_dict is not None and device not in beta1_dict:\n            beta1_dict[device] = beta1.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr, attr-defined]\n\n        device_beta1 = beta1_dict[device] if beta1_dict else beta1\n\n        # Handle complex parameters\n        if has_complex:\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                _view_as_real(\n                    device_params,\n                    device_grads,\n                    device_exp_avgs,\n                    device_exp_avg_sqs,\n                    device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n                )\n            else:\n                _view_as_real(\n                    device_params, device_grads, device_exp_avgs, device_exp_avg_sqs\n                )\n\n        # Use shared foreach utility to handle maximize\n        device_grads = handle_maximize(device_grads, maximize)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n        # Update steps using shared utility\n        update_state_steps(device_state_steps, step_size=1)\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Reuse the intermediate memory (device_grads) already allocated for maximize\n                if maximize:\n                    torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    device_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[assignment]\n                        device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n                    )\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        # Use device beta1 if beta1 is a tensor to ensure all\n        # tensors are on the same device\n        torch._foreach_lerp_(\n            device_exp_avgs, device_grads, cast(float, 1 - device_beta1)\n        )\n\n        torch._foreach_mul_(device_exp_avg_sqs, beta2)\n\n        # Due to the strictness of the _foreach_addcmul API, we can't have a single\n        # tensor scalar as the scalar arg (only python number is supported there)\n        # as a result, separate out the value mul\n        # Filed https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/139795\n        if isinstance(beta2, torch.Tensor):\n            scaled_device_grads = torch._foreach_mul(device_grads, 1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n            value = 1.0\n        else:\n            scaled_device_grads = device_grads  # type: ignore[assignment]\n            value = 1 - beta2\n\n        torch._foreach_addcmul_(\n            device_exp_avg_sqs, scaled_device_grads, device_grads, value\n        )\n\n        # Delete the local intermediate(s) since they won't be used anymore to save on peak memory\n        del device_grads\n        del scaled_device_grads\n\n        bias_correction1: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2_sqrt: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n\n        if capturable:\n            bias_correction1 = torch._foreach_pow(beta1, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            bias_correction2 = torch._foreach_pow(beta2, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            # foreach_sub doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction1, 1)\n            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction2, 1)\n            # we do not negate bias_correction1 as it'll need to be negated later anyway\n            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\n\n            # foreach_div doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n            torch._foreach_div_(bias_correction1, lr)\n            torch._foreach_reciprocal_(bias_correction1)\n\n            torch._foreach_sqrt_(bias_correction2)\n\n            # Re-assign for clarity as we maintain minimal intermediates: we'll have\n            # step_size = - lr / (1 - beta1 ^ t) where t = num_steps\n            # bias_correction2_sqrt = sqrt(1 - beta2 ^ t)\n            step_size = bias_correction1\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n                # Set intermediate to the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient when amsgrad\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, step_size)\n\n            # at this point, exp_avg_sq_sqrt = - (1 - beta^t) * [sqrt(exp_avg_sq / (1 - beta2^t)) + eps] / lr\n            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(device_params, device_exp_avgs, exp_avg_sq_sqrt)\n        else:\n            bias_correction1 = [\n                1 - beta1 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n            ]\n            bias_correction2 = [\n                1 - beta2 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n            ]\n\n            step_size = _stack_if_compiling([(lr / bc) * -1 for bc in bias_correction1])\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = [bc**0.5 for bc in bias_correction2]  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(\n                device_params,\n                device_exp_avgs,\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt,\n                step_size,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            )\n\n\ndef _fused_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,  #   .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n    else:\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n    else:\n        beta1_dict = None\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n\n            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n            key = (device, dtype)\n            if key not in beta1_dict:\n                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # Created: `torch/optim/_foreach.py`\n\nA new shared module containing common foreach optimization utilities:\n\n#### Functions Provided:\n\n1. **`handle_maximize(grads: list[Tensor], maximize: bool) -> list[Tensor]`**\n   - Handles gradient negation when maximize flag is True\n   - Eliminates duplicated maximize logic across optimizers\n   - Used in: SGD, Adam (and by extension AdamW)\n\n2. **`update_state_steps(state_steps: list[Tensor], step_size: Union[int, float, Tensor]) -> None`**\n   - Efficiently updates optimizer state steps\n   - Optimizes CPU tensor updates by pre-wrapping step values\n   - Avoids repeated tensor wrapping in foreach fallback path\n   - Used in: Adam\n\n3. **`get_device_tensor(tensor: Optional[Tensor], device: torch.device, device_dict) -> Optional[Tensor]`**\n   - Moves tensors to specific devices with caching\n   - Prevents redundant device transfers\n   - Available for future optimizer use\n\n4. **`init_device_dict(tensor: Optional[Tensor]) -> dict`**\n   - Initializes device cache dictionaries\n   - Seed dictionaries with initial tensor values\n   - Available for future optimizer use\n\n### 2. Updated: `torch/optim/sgd.py`\n\n**Changes:**\n- Added import: `from ._foreach import handle_maximize`\n- Replaced manual maximize handling: \n  ```python\n  # Old: if maximize: device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)\n  # New: device_grads = handle_maximize(device_grads, maximize)\n  ```\n- Line 418 in `_multi_tensor_sgd()` now uses shared function\n\n**Benefits:**\n- Reduced code duplication\n- Consistent maximize handling across all optimizers\n- Easier to update maximize logic in one place\n\n### 3. Created: `torch/optim/_foreach.py`\n\nA new shared module containing common foreach optimization utilities:\n\n#### Functions Provided:\n\n1. **`handle_maximize(grads: list[Tensor], maximize: bool) -> list[Tensor]`**\n   - Handles gradient negation when maximize flag is True\n   - Eliminates duplicated maximize logic across optimizers\n   - Used in: SGD, Adam (and by extension AdamW)\n\n2. **`update_state_steps(state_steps: list[Tensor], step_size: Union[int, float, Tensor]) -> None`**\n   - Efficiently updates optimizer state steps\n   - Optimizes CPU tensor updates by pre-wrapping step values\n   - Avoids repeated tensor wrapping in foreach fallback path\n   - Used in: Adam\n\n3. **`get_device_tensor(tensor: Optional[Tensor], device: torch.device, device_dict) -> Optional[Tensor]`**\n   - Moves tensors to specific devices with caching\n   - Prevents redundant device transfers\n   - Available for future optimizer use\n\n4. **`init_device_dict(tensor: Optional[Tensor]) -> dict`**\n   - Initializes device cache dictionaries\n   - Seed dictionaries with initial tensor values\n   - Available for future optimizer use\n\n### 2. Updated: `torch/optim/sgd.py`\n\n**Changes:**\n- Added import: `from ._foreach import handle_maximize`\n- Replaced manual maximize handling: \n  ```python\n  # Old: if maximize: device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)\n  # New: device_grads = handle_maximize(device_grads, maximize)\n  ```\n- Line 418 in `_multi_tensor_sgd()` now uses shared function\n\n**Benefits:**\n- Reduced code duplication\n- Consistent maximize handling across all optimizers\n- Easier to update maximize logic in one place\n\n### 3.
